00696 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject *__Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(PyObject *o, PyObject* j) {
00697     PyObject *r;
00698     if (!j) return NULL;
00699     r = PyObject_GetItem(o, j);
00700     Py_DECREF(j);
00701     return r;
00702 }
00703 
00704 
00705 #define __Pyx_GetItemInt_List(o, i, size, to_py_func) (((size) <= sizeof(Py_ssize_t)) ? \
00706                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_List_Fast(o, i) : \
00707                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, to_py_func(i)))
00708 
00709 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject *__Pyx_GetItemInt_List_Fast(PyObject *o, Py_ssize_t i) {
00710     if (likely(o != Py_None)) {
00711         if (likely((0 <= i) & (i < PyList_GET_SIZE(o)))) {
00712             PyObject *r = PyList_GET_ITEM(o, i);
00713             Py_INCREF(r);
00714             return r;
00715         }
00716         else if ((-PyList_GET_SIZE(o) <= i) & (i < 0)) {
00717             PyObject *r = PyList_GET_ITEM(o, PyList_GET_SIZE(o) + i);
00718             Py_INCREF(r);
00719             return r;
00720         }
00721     }
00722     return __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, PyInt_FromSsize_t(i));
00723 }
00724 
00725 #define __Pyx_GetItemInt_Tuple(o, i, size, to_py_func) (((size) <= sizeof(Py_ssize_t)) ? \
00726                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Tuple_Fast(o, i) : \
00727                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, to_py_func(i)))
00728 
00729 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject *__Pyx_GetItemInt_Tuple_Fast(PyObject *o, Py_ssize_t i) {
00730     if (likely(o != Py_None)) {
00731         if (likely((0 <= i) & (i < PyTuple_GET_SIZE(o)))) {
00732             PyObject *r = PyTuple_GET_ITEM(o, i);
00733             Py_INCREF(r);
00734             return r;
00735         }
00736         else if ((-PyTuple_GET_SIZE(o) <= i) & (i < 0)) {
00737             PyObject *r = PyTuple_GET_ITEM(o, PyTuple_GET_SIZE(o) + i);
00738             Py_INCREF(r);
00739             return r;
00740         }
00741     }
00742     return __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, PyInt_FromSsize_t(i));
00743 }
00744 
00745 
00746 #define __Pyx_GetItemInt(o, i, size, to_py_func) (((size) <= sizeof(Py_ssize_t)) ? \
00747                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Fast(o, i) : \
00748                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, to_py_func(i)))
00749 
00750 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject *__Pyx_GetItemInt_Fast(PyObject *o, Py_ssize_t i) {
00751     PyObject *r;
00752     if (PyList_CheckExact(o) && ((0 <= i) & (i < PyList_GET_SIZE(o)))) {
00753         r = PyList_GET_ITEM(o, i);
00754         Py_INCREF(r);
00755     }
00756     else if (PyTuple_CheckExact(o) && ((0 <= i) & (i < PyTuple_GET_SIZE(o)))) {
00757         r = PyTuple_GET_ITEM(o, i);
00758         Py_INCREF(r);
00759     }
00760     else if (Py_TYPE(o)->tp_as_sequence && Py_TYPE(o)->tp_as_sequence->sq_item && (likely(i >= 0))) {
00761         r = PySequence_GetItem(o, i);
00762     }
00763     else {
00764         r = __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, PyInt_FromSsize_t(i));
00765     }
00766     return r;
00767 }

06414   __Pyx_XDECREF(__pyx_t_2);
06415   if (__pyx_m) {
06416     __Pyx_AddTraceback("init spectralTools", __pyx_clineno, __pyx_lineno, __pyx_filename);
06417     Py_DECREF(__pyx_m); __pyx_m = 0;
06418   } else if (!PyErr_Occurred()) {
06419     PyErr_SetString(PyExc_ImportError, "init spectralTools");
06420   }
06421   __pyx_L0:;
06422   __Pyx_RefNannyFinishContext();
06423   #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
06424   return;
06425   #else
06426   return __pyx_m;
06427   #endif
06428 }
06429 
06430 /* Runtime support code */
06431 
06432 #if CYTHON_REFNANNY
06433 static __Pyx_RefNannyAPIStruct *__Pyx_RefNannyImportAPI(const char *modname) {
06434     PyObject *m = NULL, *p = NULL;
06435     void *r = NULL;
06436     m = PyImport_ImportModule((char *)modname);
06437     if (!m) goto end;
06438     p = PyObject_GetAttrString(m, (char *)"RefNannyAPI");
06439     if (!p) goto end;
06440     r = PyLong_AsVoidPtr(p);
06441 end:
06442     Py_XDECREF(p);
06443     Py_XDECREF(m);
06444     return (__Pyx_RefNannyAPIStruct *)r;
06445 }
06446 #endif /* CYTHON_REFNANNY */
06447 
06448 static PyObject *__Pyx_GetName(PyObject *dict, PyObject *name) {
06449     PyObject *result;
06450     result = PyObject_GetAttr(dict, name);
06451     if (!result) {
06452         if (dict != __pyx_b) {
06453             PyErr_Clear();
06454             result = PyObject_GetAttr(__pyx_b, name);
06455         }
06456         if (!result) {
06457             PyErr_SetObject(PyExc_NameError, name);
06458         }
06459     }
06460     return result;
06461 }
06462 
06463 static void __Pyx_RaiseArgtupleInvalid(
06464     const char* func_name,
06465     int exact,
06466     Py_ssize_t num_min,
06467     Py_ssize_t num_max,
06468     Py_ssize_t num_found)
06469 {
06470     Py_ssize_t num_expected;
06471     const char *more_or_less;
06472 
06473     if (num_found < num_min) {
06474         num_expected = num_min;
06475         more_or_less = "at least";
06476     } else {
06477         num_expected = num_max;
06478         more_or_less = "at most";
06479     }
06480     if (exact) {
06481         more_or_less = "exactly";
06482     }
06483     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
06484                  "%s() takes %s %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d positional argument%s (%"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d given)",
06485                  func_name, more_or_less, num_expected,
06486                  (num_expected == 1) ? "" : "s", num_found);
06487 }
06488 
06489 static void __Pyx_RaiseDoubleKeywordsError(
06490     const char* func_name,
06491     PyObject* kw_name)
06492 {
06493     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
06494         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
06495         "%s() got multiple values for keyword argument '%U'", func_name, kw_name);
06496         #else
06497         "%s() got multiple values for keyword argument '%s'", func_name,
06498         PyString_AS_STRING(kw_name));
06499         #endif
06500 }
06501 
06502 static int __Pyx_ParseOptionalKeywords(
06503     PyObject *kwds,
06504     PyObject **argnames[],
06505     PyObject *kwds2,
06506     PyObject *values[],
06507     Py_ssize_t num_pos_args,
06508     const char* function_name)
06509 {
06510     PyObject *key = 0, *value = 0;
06511     Py_ssize_t pos = 0;
06512     PyObject*** name;
06513     PyObject*** first_kw_arg = argnames + num_pos_args;
06514 
06515     while (PyDict_Next(kwds, &pos, &key, &value)) {
06516         name = first_kw_arg;
06517         while (*name && (**name != key)) name++;
06518         if (*name) {
06519             values[name-argnames] = value;
06520         } else {
06521             #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
06522             if (unlikely(!PyString_CheckExact(key)) && unlikely(!PyString_Check(key))) {
06523             #else
06524             if (unlikely(!PyUnicode_CheckExact(key)) && unlikely(!PyUnicode_Check(key))) {
06525             #endif
06526                 goto invalid_keyword_type;
06527             } else {
06528                 for (name = first_kw_arg; *name; name++) {
06529                     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
06530                     if (PyUnicode_GET_SIZE(**name) == PyUnicode_GET_SIZE(key) &&
06531                         PyUnicode_Compare(**name, key) == 0) break;
06532                     #else
06533                     if (PyString_GET_SIZE(**name) == PyString_GET_SIZE(key) &&
06534                         _PyString_Eq(**name, key)) break;
06535                     #endif
06536                 }
06537                 if (*name) {
06538                     values[name-argnames] = value;
06539                 } else {
06540                     /* unexpected keyword found */
06541                     for (name=argnames; name != first_kw_arg; name++) {
06542                         if (**name == key) goto arg_passed_twice;
06543                         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
06544                         if (PyUnicode_GET_SIZE(**name) == PyUnicode_GET_SIZE(key) &&
06545                             PyUnicode_Compare(**name, key) == 0) goto arg_passed_twice;
06546                         #else
06547                         if (PyString_GET_SIZE(**name) == PyString_GET_SIZE(key) &&
06548                             _PyString_Eq(**name, key)) goto arg_passed_twice;
06549                         #endif
06550                     }
06551                     if (kwds2) {
06552                         if (unlikely(PyDict_SetItem(kwds2, key, value))) goto bad;
06553                     } else {
06554                         goto invalid_keyword;
06555                     }
06556                 }
06557             }
06558         }
06559     }
06560     return 0;
06561 arg_passed_twice:
06562     __Pyx_RaiseDoubleKeywordsError(function_name, **name);
06563     goto bad;
06564 invalid_keyword_type:
06565     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
06566         "%s() keywords must be strings", function_name);
06567     goto bad;
06568 invalid_keyword:
06569     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
06570     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
06571         "%s() got an unexpected keyword argument '%s'",
06572         function_name, PyString_AsString(key));
06573     #else
06574         "%s() got an unexpected keyword argument '%U'",
06575         function_name, key);
06576     #endif
06577 bad:
06578     return -1;
06579 }
06580 
06581 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_TypeTest(PyObject *obj, PyTypeObject *type) {
06582     if (unlikely(!type)) {
06583         PyErr_Format(PyExc_SystemError, "Missing type object");
06584         return 0;
06585     }
06586     if (likely(PyObject_TypeCheck(obj, type)))
06587         return 1;
06588     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError, "Cannot convert %.200s to %.200s",
06589                  Py_TYPE(obj)->tp_name, type->tp_name);
06590     return 0;
06591 }
06592 
06593 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_IsLittleEndian(void) {
06594   unsigned int n = 1;
06595   return *(unsigned char*)(&n) != 0;
06596 }
06597 
06598 typedef struct {
06599   __Pyx_StructField root;
06600   __Pyx_BufFmt_StackElem* head;
06601   size_t fmt_offset;
06602   size_t new_count, enc_count;
06603   int is_complex;
06604   char enc_type;
06605   char new_packmode;
06606   char enc_packmode;
06607 } __Pyx_BufFmt_Context;
06608 
06609 static void __Pyx_BufFmt_Init(__Pyx_BufFmt_Context* ctx,
06610                               __Pyx_BufFmt_StackElem* stack,
06611                               __Pyx_TypeInfo* type) {
06612   stack[0].field = &ctx->root;
06613   stack[0].parent_offset = 0;
06614   ctx->root.type = type;
06615   ctx->root.name = "buffer dtype";
06616   ctx->root.offset = 0;
06617   ctx->head = stack;
06618   ctx->head->field = &ctx->root;
06619   ctx->fmt_offset = 0;
06620   ctx->head->parent_offset = 0;
06621   ctx->new_packmode = '@';
06622   ctx->enc_packmode = '@';
06623   ctx->new_count = 1;
06624   ctx->enc_count = 0;
06625   ctx->enc_type = 0;
06626   ctx->is_complex = 0;
06627   while (type->typegroup == 'S') {
06628     ++ctx->head;
06629     ctx->head->field = type->fields;
06630     ctx->head->parent_offset = 0;
06631     type = type->fields->type;
06632   }
06633 }
06634 
06635 static int __Pyx_BufFmt_ParseNumber(const char** ts) {
06636     int count;
06637     const char* t = *ts;
06638     if (*t < '0' || *t > '9') {
06639       return -1;
06640     } else {
06641         count = *t++ - '0';
06642         while (*t >= '0' && *t < '9') {
06643             count *= 10;
06644             count += *t++ - '0';
06645         }
06646     }
06647     *ts = t;
06648     return count;
06649 }
06650 
06651 static void __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseUnexpectedChar(char ch) {
06652   PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
06653                "Unexpected format string character: '%c'", ch);
06654 }
06655 
06656 static const char* __Pyx_BufFmt_DescribeTypeChar(char ch, int is_complex) {
06657   switch (ch) {
06658     case 'b': return "'char'";
06659     case 'B': return "'unsigned char'";
06660     case 'h': return "'short'";
06661     case 'H': return "'unsigned short'";
06662     case 'i': return "'int'";
06663     case 'I': return "'unsigned int'";
06664     case 'l': return "'long'";
06665     case 'L': return "'unsigned long'";
06666     case 'q': return "'long long'";
06667     case 'Q': return "'unsigned long long'";
06668     case 'f': return (is_complex ? "'complex float'" : "'float'");
06669     case 'd': return (is_complex ? "'complex double'" : "'double'");
06670     case 'g': return (is_complex ? "'complex long double'" : "'long double'");
06671     case 'T': return "a struct";
06672     case 'O': return "Python object";
06673     case 'P': return "a pointer";
06674     case 0: return "end";
06675     default: return "unparseable format string";
06676   }
06677 }
06678 
06679 static size_t __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToStandardSize(char ch, int is_complex) {
06680   switch (ch) {
06681     case '?': case 'c': case 'b': case 'B': return 1;
06682     case 'h': case 'H': return 2;
06683     case 'i': case 'I': case 'l': case 'L': return 4;
06684     case 'q': case 'Q': return 8;
06685     case 'f': return (is_complex ? 8 : 4);
06686     case 'd': return (is_complex ? 16 : 8);
06687     case 'g': {
06688       PyErr_SetString(PyExc_ValueError, "Python does not define a standard format string size for long double ('g')..");
06689       return 0;
06690     }
06691     case 'O': case 'P': return sizeof(void*);
06692     default:
06693       __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseUnexpectedChar(ch);
06694       return 0;
06695     }
06696 }
06697 
06698 static size_t __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToNativeSize(char ch, int is_complex) {
06699   switch (ch) {
06700     case 'c': case 'b': case 'B': return 1;
06701     case 'h': case 'H': return sizeof(short);
06702     case 'i': case 'I': return sizeof(int);
06703     case 'l': case 'L': return sizeof(long);
06704     #ifdef HAVE_LONG_LONG
06705     case 'q': case 'Q': return sizeof(PY_LONG_LONG);
06706     #endif
06707     case 'f': return sizeof(float) * (is_complex ? 2 : 1);
06708     case 'd': return sizeof(double) * (is_complex ? 2 : 1);
06709     case 'g': return sizeof(long double) * (is_complex ? 2 : 1);
06710     case 'O': case 'P': return sizeof(void*);
06711     default: {
06712       __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseUnexpectedChar(ch);
06713       return 0;
06714     }
06715   }
06716 }
06717 
06718 typedef struct { char c; short x; } __Pyx_st_short;
06719 typedef struct { char c; int x; } __Pyx_st_int;
06720 typedef struct { char c; long x; } __Pyx_st_long;
06721 typedef struct { char c; float x; } __Pyx_st_float;
06722 typedef struct { char c; double x; } __Pyx_st_double;
06723 typedef struct { char c; long double x; } __Pyx_st_longdouble;
06724 typedef struct { char c; void *x; } __Pyx_st_void_p;
06725 #ifdef HAVE_LONG_LONG
06726 typedef struct { char c; PY_LONG_LONG x; } __Pyx_st_longlong;
06727 #endif
06728 
06729 static size_t __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToAlignment(char ch, int is_complex) {
06730   switch (ch) {
06731     case '?': case 'c': case 'b': case 'B': return 1;
06732     case 'h': case 'H': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_short) - sizeof(short);
06733     case 'i': case 'I': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_int) - sizeof(int);
06734     case 'l': case 'L': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_long) - sizeof(long);
06735 #ifdef HAVE_LONG_LONG
06736     case 'q': case 'Q': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_longlong) - sizeof(PY_LONG_LONG);
06737 #endif
06738     case 'f': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_float) - sizeof(float);
06739     case 'd': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_double) - sizeof(double);
06740     case 'g': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_longdouble) - sizeof(long double);
06741     case 'P': case 'O': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_void_p) - sizeof(void*);
06742     default:
06743       __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseUnexpectedChar(ch);
06744       return 0;
06745     }
06746 }
06747 
06748 static char __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToGroup(char ch, int is_complex) {
06749   switch (ch) {
06750     case 'c': case 'b': case 'h': case 'i': case 'l': case 'q': return 'I';
06751     case 'B': case 'H': case 'I': case 'L': case 'Q': return 'U';
06752     case 'f': case 'd': case 'g': return (is_complex ? 'C' : 'R');
06753     case 'O': return 'O';
06754     case 'P': return 'P';
06755     default: {
06756       __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseUnexpectedChar(ch);
06757       return 0;
06758     }
06759   }
06760 }
06761 
06762 static void __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseExpected(__Pyx_BufFmt_Context* ctx) {
06763   if (ctx->head == NULL || ctx->head->field == &ctx->root) {
06764     const char* expected;
06765     const char* quote;
06766     if (ctx->head == NULL) {
06767       expected = "end";
06768       quote = "";
06769     } else {
06770       expected = ctx->head->field->type->name;
06771       quote = "'";
06772     }
06773     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
06774                  "Buffer dtype mismatch, expected %s%s%s but got %s",
06775                  quote, expected, quote,
06776                  __Pyx_BufFmt_DescribeTypeChar(ctx->enc_type, ctx->is_complex));
06777   } else {
06778     __Pyx_StructField* field = ctx->head->field;
06779     __Pyx_StructField* parent = (ctx->head - 1)->field;
06780     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
06781                  "Buffer dtype mismatch, expected '%s' but got %s in '%s.%s'",
06782                  field->type->name, __Pyx_BufFmt_DescribeTypeChar(ctx->enc_type, ctx->is_complex),
06783                  parent->type->name, field->name);
06784   }
06785 }
06786 
06787 static int __Pyx_BufFmt_ProcessTypeChunk(__Pyx_BufFmt_Context* ctx) {
06788   char group;
06789   size_t size, offset;
06790   if (ctx->enc_type == 0) return 0;
06791   group = __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToGroup(ctx->enc_type, ctx->is_complex);
06792   do {
06793     __Pyx_StructField* field = ctx->head->field;
06794     __Pyx_TypeInfo* type = field->type;
06795 
06796     if (ctx->enc_packmode == '@' || ctx->enc_packmode == '^') {
06797       size = __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToNativeSize(ctx->enc_type, ctx->is_complex);
06798     } else {
06799       size = __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToStandardSize(ctx->enc_type, ctx->is_complex);
06800     }
06801     if (ctx->enc_packmode == '@') {
06802       size_t align_at = __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToAlignment(ctx->enc_type, ctx->is_complex);
06803       size_t align_mod_offset;
06804       if (align_at == 0) return -1;
06805       align_mod_offset = ctx->fmt_offset % align_at;
06806       if (align_mod_offset > 0) ctx->fmt_offset += align_at - align_mod_offset;
06807     }
06808 
06809     if (type->size != size || type->typegroup != group) {
06810       if (type->typegroup == 'C' && type->fields != NULL) {
06811         /* special case -- treat as struct rather than complex number */
06812         size_t parent_offset = ctx->head->parent_offset + field->offset;
06813         ++ctx->head;
06814         ctx->head->field = type->fields;
06815         ctx->head->parent_offset = parent_offset;
06816         continue;
06817       }
06818 
06819       __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseExpected(ctx);
06820       return -1;
06821     }
06822 
06823     offset = ctx->head->parent_offset + field->offset;
06824     if (ctx->fmt_offset != offset) {
06825       PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
06826                    "Buffer dtype mismatch; next field is at offset %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d but %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d expected",
06827                    (Py_ssize_t)ctx->fmt_offset, (Py_ssize_t)offset);
06828       return -1;
06829     }
06830 
06831     ctx->fmt_offset += size;
06832 
06833     --ctx->enc_count; /* Consume from buffer string */
06834 
06835     /* Done checking, move to next field, pushing or popping struct stack if needed */
06836     while (1) {
06837       if (field == &ctx->root) {
06838         ctx->head = NULL;
06839         if (ctx->enc_count != 0) {
06840           __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseExpected(ctx);
06841           return -1;
06842         }
06843         break; /* breaks both loops as ctx->enc_count == 0 */
06844       }
06845       ctx->head->field = ++field;
06846       if (field->type == NULL) {
06847         --ctx->head;
06848         field = ctx->head->field;
06849         continue;
06850       } else if (field->type->typegroup == 'S') {
06851         size_t parent_offset = ctx->head->parent_offset + field->offset;
06852         if (field->type->fields->type == NULL) continue; /* empty struct */
06853         field = field->type->fields;
06854         ++ctx->head;
06855         ctx->head->field = field;
06856         ctx->head->parent_offset = parent_offset;
06857         break;
06858       } else {
06859         break;
06860       }
06861     }
06862   } while (ctx->enc_count);
06863   ctx->enc_type = 0;
06864   ctx->is_complex = 0;
06865   return 0;
06866 }
06867 
06868 static const char* __Pyx_BufFmt_CheckString(__Pyx_BufFmt_Context* ctx, const char* ts) {
06869   int got_Z = 0;
06870   while (1) {
06871     switch(*ts) {
06872       case 0:
06873         if (ctx->enc_type != 0 && ctx->head == NULL) {
06874           __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseExpected(ctx);
06875           return NULL;
06876         }
06877         if (__Pyx_BufFmt_ProcessTypeChunk(ctx) == -1) return NULL;
06878         if (ctx->head != NULL) {
06879           __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseExpected(ctx);
06880           return NULL;
06881         }
06882         return ts;
06883       case ' ':
06884       case 10:
06885       case 13:
06886         ++ts;
06887         break;
06888       case '<':
06889         if (!__Pyx_IsLittleEndian()) {
06890           PyErr_SetString(PyExc_ValueError, "Little-endian buffer not supported on big-endian compiler");
06891           return NULL;
06892         }
06893         ctx->new_packmode = '=';
06894         ++ts;
06895         break;
06896       case '>':
06897       case '!':
06898         if (__Pyx_IsLittleEndian()) {
06899           PyErr_SetString(PyExc_ValueError, "Big-endian buffer not supported on little-endian compiler");
06900           return NULL;
06901         }
06902         ctx->new_packmode = '=';
06903         ++ts;
06904         break;
06905       case '=':
06906       case '@':
06907       case '^':
06908         ctx->new_packmode = *ts++;
06909         break;
06910       case 'T': /* substruct */
06911         {
06912           const char* ts_after_sub;
06913           size_t i, struct_count = ctx->new_count;
06914           ctx->new_count = 1;
06915           ++ts;
06916           if (*ts != '{') {
06917             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_ValueError, "Buffer acquisition: Expected '{' after 'T'");
06918             return NULL;
06919           }
06920           ++ts;
06921           ts_after_sub = ts;
06922           for (i = 0; i != struct_count; ++i) {
06923             ts_after_sub = __Pyx_BufFmt_CheckString(ctx, ts);
06924             if (!ts_after_sub) return NULL;
06925           }
06926           ts = ts_after_sub;
06927         }
06928         break;
06929       case '}': /* end of substruct; either repeat or move on */
06930         ++ts;
06931         return ts;
06932       case 'x':
06933         if (__Pyx_BufFmt_ProcessTypeChunk(ctx) == -1) return NULL;
06934         ctx->fmt_offset += ctx->new_count;
06935         ctx->new_count = 1;
06936         ctx->enc_count = 0;
06937         ctx->enc_type = 0;
06938         ctx->enc_packmode = ctx->new_packmode;
06939         ++ts;
06940         break;
06941       case 'Z':
06942         got_Z = 1;
06943         ++ts;
06944         if (*ts != 'f' && *ts != 'd' && *ts != 'g') {
06945           __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseUnexpectedChar('Z');
06946           return NULL;
06947         }        /* fall through */
06948       case 'c': case 'b': case 'B': case 'h': case 'H': case 'i': case 'I':
06949       case 'l': case 'L': case 'q': case 'Q':
06950       case 'f': case 'd': case 'g':
06951       case 'O':
06952         if (ctx->enc_type == *ts && got_Z == ctx->is_complex &&
06953             ctx->enc_packmode == ctx->new_packmode) {
06954           /* Continue pooling same type */
06955           ctx->enc_count += ctx->new_count;
06956         } else {
06957           /* New type */
06958           if (__Pyx_BufFmt_ProcessTypeChunk(ctx) == -1) return NULL;
06959           ctx->enc_count = ctx->new_count;
06960           ctx->enc_packmode = ctx->new_packmode;
06961           ctx->enc_type = *ts;
06962           ctx->is_complex = got_Z;
06963         }
06964         ++ts;
06965         ctx->new_count = 1;
06966         got_Z = 0;
06967         break;
06968       case ':':
06969         ++ts;
06970         while(*ts != ':') ++ts;
06971         ++ts;
06972         break;
06973       default:
06974         {
06975           int number = __Pyx_BufFmt_ParseNumber(&ts);
06976           if (number == -1) { /* First char was not a digit */
06977             PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
06978                          "Does not understand character buffer dtype format string ('%c')", *ts);
06979             return NULL;
06980           }
06981           ctx->new_count = (size_t)number; 
06982         }
06983     }
06984   }
06985 }
06986 
06987 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_ZeroBuffer(Py_buffer* buf) {
06988   buf->buf = NULL;
06989   buf->obj = NULL;
06990   buf->strides = __Pyx_zeros;
06991   buf->shape = __Pyx_zeros;
06992   buf->suboffsets = __Pyx_minusones;
06993 }
06994 
06995 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_GetBufferAndValidate(Py_buffer* buf, PyObject* obj, __Pyx_TypeInfo* dtype, int flags, int nd, int cast, __Pyx_BufFmt_StackElem* stack) {
06996   if (obj == Py_None || obj == NULL) {
06997     __Pyx_ZeroBuffer(buf);
06998     return 0;
06999   }
07000   buf->buf = NULL;
07001   if (__Pyx_GetBuffer(obj, buf, flags) == -1) goto fail;
07002   if (buf->ndim != nd) {
07003     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
07004                  "Buffer has wrong number of dimensions (expected %d, got %d)",
07005                  nd, buf->ndim);
07006     goto fail;
07007   }
07008   if (!cast) {
07009     __Pyx_BufFmt_Context ctx;
07010     __Pyx_BufFmt_Init(&ctx, stack, dtype);
07011     if (!__Pyx_BufFmt_CheckString(&ctx, buf->format)) goto fail;
07012   }
07013   if ((unsigned)buf->itemsize != dtype->size) {
07014     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
07015       "Item size of buffer (%"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d byte%s) does not match size of '%s' (%"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d byte%s)",
07016       buf->itemsize, (buf->itemsize > 1) ? "s" : "",
07017       dtype->name, (Py_ssize_t)dtype->size, (dtype->size > 1) ? "s" : "");
07018     goto fail;
07019   }
07020   if (buf->suboffsets == NULL) buf->suboffsets = __Pyx_minusones;
07021   return 0;
07022 fail:;
07023   __Pyx_ZeroBuffer(buf);
07024   return -1;
07025 }
07026 
07027 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_SafeReleaseBuffer(Py_buffer* info) {
07028   if (info->buf == NULL) return;
07029   if (info->suboffsets == __Pyx_minusones) info->suboffsets = NULL;
07030   __Pyx_ReleaseBuffer(info);
07031 }
07032 
07033 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_ErrRestore(PyObject *type, PyObject *value, PyObject *tb) {
07034     PyObject *tmp_type, *tmp_value, *tmp_tb;
07035     PyThreadState *tstate = PyThreadState_GET();
07036 
07037     tmp_type = tstate->curexc_type;
07038     tmp_value = tstate->curexc_value;
07039     tmp_tb = tstate->curexc_traceback;
07040     tstate->curexc_type = type;
07041     tstate->curexc_value = value;
07042     tstate->curexc_traceback = tb;
07043     Py_XDECREF(tmp_type);
07044     Py_XDECREF(tmp_value);
07045     Py_XDECREF(tmp_tb);
07046 }
07047 
07048 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_ErrFetch(PyObject **type, PyObject **value, PyObject **tb) {
07049     PyThreadState *tstate = PyThreadState_GET();
07050     *type = tstate->curexc_type;
07051     *value = tstate->curexc_value;
07052     *tb = tstate->curexc_traceback;
07053 
07054     tstate->curexc_type = 0;
07055     tstate->curexc_value = 0;
07056     tstate->curexc_traceback = 0;
07057 }
07058 
07059 
07060 
07061 static double __Pyx__PyObject_AsDouble(PyObject* obj) {
07062     PyObject* float_value;
07063     if (Py_TYPE(obj)->tp_as_number && Py_TYPE(obj)->tp_as_number->nb_float) {
07064         return PyFloat_AsDouble(obj);
07065     } else if (PyUnicode_CheckExact(obj) || PyBytes_CheckExact(obj)) {
07066 #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
07067         float_value = PyFloat_FromString(obj);
07068 #else
07069         float_value = PyFloat_FromString(obj, 0);
07070 #endif
07071     } else {
07072         PyObject* args = PyTuple_New(1);
07073         if (unlikely(!args)) goto bad;
07074         PyTuple_SET_ITEM(args, 0, obj);
07075         float_value = PyObject_Call((PyObject*)&PyFloat_Type, args, 0);
07076         PyTuple_SET_ITEM(args, 0, 0);
07077         Py_DECREF(args);
07078     }
07079     if (likely(float_value)) {
07080         double value = PyFloat_AS_DOUBLE(float_value);
07081         Py_DECREF(float_value);
07082         return value;
07083     }
07084 bad:
07085     return (double)-1;
07086 }
07087 
07088 static CYTHON_INLINE long __Pyx_div_long(long a, long b) {
07089     long q = a / b;
07090     long r = a - q*b;
07091     q -= ((r != 0) & ((r ^ b) < 0));
07092     return q;
07093 }
07094 
07095 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_RaiseNeedMoreValuesError(Py_ssize_t index) {
07096     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
07097                  "need more than %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d value%s to unpack",
07098                  index, (index == 1) ? "" : "s");
07099 }
07100 
07101 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_RaiseTooManyValuesError(Py_ssize_t expected) {
07102     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
07103                  "too many values to unpack (expected %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d)", expected);
07104 }
07105 
07106 static int __Pyx_IternextUnpackEndCheck(PyObject *retval, Py_ssize_t expected) {
07107     if (unlikely(retval)) {
07108         Py_DECREF(retval);
07109         __Pyx_RaiseTooManyValuesError(expected);
07110         return -1;
07111     } else if (PyErr_Occurred()) {
07112         if (likely(PyErr_ExceptionMatches(PyExc_StopIteration))) {
07113             PyErr_Clear();
07114             return 0;
07115         } else {
07116             return -1;
07117         }
07118     }
07119     return 0;
07120 }
07121 
07122 #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
07123 static void __Pyx_Raise(PyObject *type, PyObject *value, PyObject *tb, PyObject *cause) {
07124     /* cause is unused */
07125     Py_XINCREF(type);
07126     Py_XINCREF(value);
07127     Py_XINCREF(tb);
07128     /* First, check the traceback argument, replacing None with NULL. */
07129     if (tb == Py_None) {
07130         Py_DECREF(tb);
07131         tb = 0;
07132     }
07133     else if (tb != NULL && !PyTraceBack_Check(tb)) {
07134         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
07135             "raise: arg 3 must be a traceback or None");
07136         goto raise_error;
07137     }
07138     /* Next, replace a missing value with None */
07139     if (value == NULL) {
07140         value = Py_None;
07141         Py_INCREF(value);
07142     }
07143     #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
07144     if (!PyClass_Check(type))
07145     #else
07146     if (!PyType_Check(type))
07147     #endif
07148     {
07149         /* Raising an instance.  The value should be a dummy. */
07150         if (value != Py_None) {
07151             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
07152                 "instance exception may not have a separate value");
07153             goto raise_error;
07154         }
07155         /* Normalize to raise <class>, <instance> */
07156         Py_DECREF(value);
07157         value = type;
07158         #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
07159             if (PyInstance_Check(type)) {
07160                 type = (PyObject*) ((PyInstanceObject*)type)->in_class;
07161                 Py_INCREF(type);
07162             }
07163             else {
07164                 type = 0;
07165                 PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
07166                     "raise: exception must be an old-style class or instance");
07167                 goto raise_error;
07168             }
07169         #else
07170             type = (PyObject*) Py_TYPE(type);
07171             Py_INCREF(type);
07172             if (!PyType_IsSubtype((PyTypeObject *)type, (PyTypeObject *)PyExc_BaseException)) {
07173                 PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
07174                     "raise: exception class must be a subclass of BaseException");
07175                 goto raise_error;
07176             }
07177         #endif
07178     }
07179 
07180     __Pyx_ErrRestore(type, value, tb);
07181     return;
07182 raise_error:
07183     Py_XDECREF(value);
07184     Py_XDECREF(type);
07185     Py_XDECREF(tb);
07186     return;
07187 }
07188 
07189 #else /* Python 3+ */
07190 
07191 static void __Pyx_Raise(PyObject *type, PyObject *value, PyObject *tb, PyObject *cause) {
07192     if (tb == Py_None) {
07193         tb = 0;
07194     } else if (tb && !PyTraceBack_Check(tb)) {
07195         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
07196             "raise: arg 3 must be a traceback or None");
07197         goto bad;
07198     }
07199     if (value == Py_None)
07200         value = 0;
07201 
07202     if (PyExceptionInstance_Check(type)) {
07203         if (value) {
07204             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
07205                 "instance exception may not have a separate value");
07206             goto bad;
07207         }
07208         value = type;
07209         type = (PyObject*) Py_TYPE(value);
07210     } else if (!PyExceptionClass_Check(type)) {
07211         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
07212             "raise: exception class must be a subclass of BaseException");
07213         goto bad;
07214     }
07215 
07216     if (cause) {
07217         PyObject *fixed_cause;
07218         if (PyExceptionClass_Check(cause)) {
07219             fixed_cause = PyObject_CallObject(cause, NULL);
07220             if (fixed_cause == NULL)
07221                 goto bad;
07222         }
07223         else if (PyExceptionInstance_Check(cause)) {
07224             fixed_cause = cause;
07225             Py_INCREF(fixed_cause);
07226         }
07227         else {
07228             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
07229                             "exception causes must derive from "
07230                             "BaseException");
07231             goto bad;
07232         }
07233         if (!value) {
07234             value = PyObject_CallObject(type, NULL);
07235         }
07236         PyException_SetCause(value, fixed_cause);
07237     }
07238 
07239     PyErr_SetObject(type, value);
07240 
07241     if (tb) {
07242         PyThreadState *tstate = PyThreadState_GET();
07243         PyObject* tmp_tb = tstate->curexc_traceback;
07244         if (tb != tmp_tb) {
07245             Py_INCREF(tb);
07246             tstate->curexc_traceback = tb;
07247             Py_XDECREF(tmp_tb);
07248         }
07249     }
07250 
07251 bad:
07252     return;
07253 }
07254 #endif
07255 
07256 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_RaiseNoneNotIterableError(void) {
07257     PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError, "'NoneType' object is not iterable");
07258 }
07259 
07260 static void __Pyx_UnpackTupleError(PyObject *t, Py_ssize_t index) {
07261     if (t == Py_None) {
07262       __Pyx_RaiseNoneNotIterableError();
07263     } else if (PyTuple_GET_SIZE(t) < index) {
07264       __Pyx_RaiseNeedMoreValuesError(PyTuple_GET_SIZE(t));
07265     } else {
07266       __Pyx_RaiseTooManyValuesError(index);
07267     }
07268 }

07270 #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
07271 static int __Pyx_GetBuffer(PyObject *obj, Py_buffer *view, int flags) {
07272   #if PY_VERSION_HEX >= 0x02060000
07273   if (PyObject_CheckBuffer(obj)) return PyObject_GetBuffer(obj, view, flags);
07274   #endif
07275   if (PyObject_TypeCheck(obj, __pyx_ptype_5numpy_ndarray)) return __pyx_pf_5numpy_7ndarray___getbuffer__(obj, view, flags);
07276   else {
07277   PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError, "'%100s' does not have the buffer interface", Py_TYPE(obj)->tp_name);
07278   return -1;
07279     }
07280 }
07281 
07282 static void __Pyx_ReleaseBuffer(Py_buffer *view) {
07283   PyObject* obj = view->obj;
07284   if (obj) {
07285     #if PY_VERSION_HEX >= 0x02060000
07286     if (PyObject_CheckBuffer(obj)) {PyBuffer_Release(view); return;}
07287     #endif
07288     if (PyObject_TypeCheck(obj, __pyx_ptype_5numpy_ndarray)) __pyx_pf_5numpy_7ndarray_1__releasebuffer__(obj, view);
07289     Py_DECREF(obj);
07290     view->obj = NULL;
07291   }
07292 }
07293 
07294 #endif
07295 
07296 static PyObject *__Pyx_Import(PyObject *name, PyObject *from_list, long level) {
07297     PyObject *py_import = 0;
07298     PyObject *empty_list = 0;
07299     PyObject *module = 0;
07300     PyObject *global_dict = 0;
07301     PyObject *empty_dict = 0;
07302     PyObject *list;
07303     py_import = __Pyx_GetAttrString(__pyx_b, "__import__");
07304     if (!py_import)
07305         goto bad;
07306     if (from_list)
07307         list = from_list;
07308     else {
07309         empty_list = PyList_New(0);
07310         if (!empty_list)
07311             goto bad;
07312         list = empty_list;
07313     }
07314     global_dict = PyModule_GetDict(__pyx_m);
07315     if (!global_dict)
07316         goto bad;
07317     empty_dict = PyDict_New();
07318     if (!empty_dict)
07319         goto bad;
07320     #if PY_VERSION_HEX >= 0x02050000
07321     {
07322         PyObject *py_level = PyInt_FromLong(level);
07323         if (!py_level)
07324             goto bad;
07325         module = PyObject_CallFunctionObjArgs(py_import,
07326             name, global_dict, empty_dict, list, py_level, NULL);
07327         Py_DECREF(py_level);
07328     }
07329     #else
07330     if (level>0) {
07331         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_RuntimeError, "Relative import is not supported for Python <=2.4.");
07332         goto bad;
07333     }
07334     module = PyObject_CallFunctionObjArgs(py_import,
07335         name, global_dict, empty_dict, list, NULL);
07336     #endif
07337 bad:
07338     Py_XDECREF(empty_list);
07339     Py_XDECREF(py_import);
07340     Py_XDECREF(empty_dict);
07341     return module;
07342 }

07344 #if CYTHON_CCOMPLEX
07345   #ifdef __cplusplus
07346     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __pyx_t_float_complex_from_parts(float x, float y) {
07347       return ::std::complex< float >(x, y);
07348     }
07349   #else
07350     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __pyx_t_float_complex_from_parts(float x, float y) {
07351       return x + y*(__pyx_t_float_complex)_Complex_I;
07352     }
07353   #endif
07354 #else
07355     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __pyx_t_float_complex_from_parts(float x, float y) {

07357       z.real = x;
07358       z.imag = y;
07359       return z;
07360     }

07362 
07363 #if CYTHON_CCOMPLEX
07364 #else
07365     static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_c_eqf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
07366        return (a.real == b.real) && (a.imag == b.imag);
07367     }
07368     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_sumf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
07369         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
07370         z.real = a.real + b.real;
07371         z.imag = a.imag + b.imag;
07372         return z;
07373     }
07374     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_difff(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
07375         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
07376         z.real = a.real - b.real;
07377         z.imag = a.imag - b.imag;
07378         return z;
07379     }
07380     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_prodf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
07381         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
07382         z.real = a.real * b.real - a.imag * b.imag;
07383         z.imag = a.real * b.imag + a.imag * b.real;
07384         return z;
07385     }
07386     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_quotf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
07387         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
07388         float denom = b.real * b.real + b.imag * b.imag;
07389         z.real = (a.real * b.real + a.imag * b.imag) / denom;
07390         z.imag = (a.imag * b.real - a.real * b.imag) / denom;
07391         return z;
07392     }
07393     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_negf(__pyx_t_float_complex a) {
07394         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
07395         z.real = -a.real;
07396         z.imag = -a.imag;
07397         return z;
07398     }
07399     static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_c_is_zerof(__pyx_t_float_complex a) {
07400        return (a.real == 0) && (a.imag == 0);
07401     }
07402     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_conjf(__pyx_t_float_complex a) {
07403         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
07404         z.real =  a.real;
07405         z.imag = -a.imag;
07406         return z;
07407     }
07408     #if 1
07409         static CYTHON_INLINE float __Pyx_c_absf(__pyx_t_float_complex z) {
07410           #if !defined(HAVE_HYPOT) || defined(_MSC_VER)
07411             return sqrtf(z.real*z.real + z.imag*z.imag);
07412           #else
07413             return hypotf(z.real, z.imag);
07414           #endif
07415         }
07416         static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_powf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
07417             __pyx_t_float_complex z;
07418             float r, lnr, theta, z_r, z_theta;
07419             if (b.imag == 0 && b.real == (int)b.real) {
07420                 if (b.real < 0) {
07421                     float denom = a.real * a.real + a.imag * a.imag;
07422                     a.real = a.real / denom;
07423                     a.imag = -a.imag / denom;
07424                     b.real = -b.real;
07425                 }
07426                 switch ((int)b.real) {
07427                     case 0:
07428                         z.real = 1;
07429                         z.imag = 0;
07430                         return z;
07431                     case 1:
07432                         return a;
07433                     case 2:
07434                         z = __Pyx_c_prodf(a, a);
07435                         return __Pyx_c_prodf(a, a);
07436                     case 3:
07437                         z = __Pyx_c_prodf(a, a);
07438                         return __Pyx_c_prodf(z, a);
07439                     case 4:
07440                         z = __Pyx_c_prodf(a, a);
07441                         return __Pyx_c_prodf(z, z);
07442                 }
07443             }
07444             if (a.imag == 0) {
07445                 if (a.real == 0) {
07446                     return a;
07447                 }
07448                 r = a.real;
07449                 theta = 0;
07450             } else {
07451                 r = __Pyx_c_absf(a);
07452                 theta = atan2f(a.imag, a.real);
07453             }
07454             lnr = logf(r);
07455             z_r = expf(lnr * b.real - theta * b.imag);
07456             z_theta = theta * b.real + lnr * b.imag;
07457             z.real = z_r * cosf(z_theta);
07458             z.imag = z_r * sinf(z_theta);
07459             return z;
07460         }
07461     #endif
07462 #endif
07463 
07464 #if CYTHON_CCOMPLEX
07465   #ifdef __cplusplus
07466     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __pyx_t_double_complex_from_parts(double x, double y) {
07467       return ::std::complex< double >(x, y);
07468     }
07469   #else
07470     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __pyx_t_double_complex_from_parts(double x, double y) {
07471       return x + y*(__pyx_t_double_complex)_Complex_I;
07472     }
07473   #endif
07474 #else
07475     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __pyx_t_double_complex_from_parts(double x, double y) {
07476       __pyx_t_double_complex z;
07477       z.real = x;
07478       z.imag = y;
07479       return z;
07480     }
07481 #endif

07483 #if CYTHON_CCOMPLEX
07484 #else
07485     static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_c_eq(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
07486        return (a.real == b.real) && (a.imag == b.imag);
07487     }
07488     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_sum(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
07489         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
07490         z.real = a.real + b.real;
07491         z.imag = a.imag + b.imag;
07492         return z;
07493     }
07494     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_diff(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
07495         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
07496         z.real = a.real - b.real;
07497         z.imag = a.imag - b.imag;
07498         return z;
07499     }
07500     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_prod(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
07501         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
07502         z.real = a.real * b.real - a.imag * b.imag;
07503         z.imag = a.real * b.imag + a.imag * b.real;
07504         return z;
07505     }
07506     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_quot(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
07507         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
07508         double denom = b.real * b.real + b.imag * b.imag;
07509         z.real = (a.real * b.real + a.imag * b.imag) / denom;
07510         z.imag = (a.imag * b.real - a.real * b.imag) / denom;
07511         return z;
07512     }
07513     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_neg(__pyx_t_double_complex a) {
07514         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
07515         z.real = -a.real;
07516         z.imag = -a.imag;
07517         return z;
07518     }
07519     static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_c_is_zero(__pyx_t_double_complex a) {
07520        return (a.real == 0) && (a.imag == 0);
07521     }
07522     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_conj(__pyx_t_double_complex a) {
07523         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
07524         z.real =  a.real;
07525         z.imag = -a.imag;
07526         return z;
07527     }
07528     #if 1
07529         static CYTHON_INLINE double __Pyx_c_abs(__pyx_t_double_complex z) {
07530           #if !defined(HAVE_HYPOT) || defined(_MSC_VER)
07531             return sqrt(z.real*z.real + z.imag*z.imag);
07532           #else
07533             return hypot(z.real, z.imag);
07534           #endif
07535         }
07536         static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_pow(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
07537             __pyx_t_double_complex z;
07538             double r, lnr, theta, z_r, z_theta;
07539             if (b.imag == 0 && b.real == (int)b.real) {
07540                 if (b.real < 0) {
07541                     double denom = a.real * a.real + a.imag * a.imag;
07542                     a.real = a.real / denom;
07543                     a.imag = -a.imag / denom;
07544                     b.real = -b.real;
07545                 }
07546                 switch ((int)b.real) {
07547                     case 0:
07548                         z.real = 1;
07549                         z.imag = 0;
07550                         return z;
07551                     case 1:
07552                         return a;
07553                     case 2:
07554                         z = __Pyx_c_prod(a, a);
07555                         return __Pyx_c_prod(a, a);
07556                     case 3:
07557                         z = __Pyx_c_prod(a, a);
07558                         return __Pyx_c_prod(z, a);
07559                     case 4:
07560                         z = __Pyx_c_prod(a, a);
07561                         return __Pyx_c_prod(z, z);
07562                 }
07563             }
07564             if (a.imag == 0) {
07565                 if (a.real == 0) {
07566                     return a;
07567                 }
07568                 r = a.real;
07569                 theta = 0;
07570             } else {
07571                 r = __Pyx_c_abs(a);
07572                 theta = atan2(a.imag, a.real);
07573             }
07574             lnr = log(r);
07575             z_r = exp(lnr * b.real - theta * b.imag);
07576             z_theta = theta * b.real + lnr * b.imag;
07577             z.real = z_r * cos(z_theta);
07578             z.imag = z_r * sin(z_theta);
07579             return z;
07580         }
07581     #endif
07582 #endif
07583 
07584 static CYTHON_INLINE unsigned char __Pyx_PyInt_AsUnsignedChar(PyObject* x) {
07585     const unsigned char neg_one = (unsigned char)-1, const_zero = 0;
07586     const int is_unsigned = neg_one > const_zero;
07587     if (sizeof(unsigned char) < sizeof(long)) {
07588         long val = __Pyx_PyInt_AsLong(x);
07589         if (unlikely(val != (long)(unsigned char)val)) {
07590             if (!unlikely(val == -1 && PyErr_Occurred())) {
07591                 PyErr_SetString(PyExc_OverflowError,
07592                     (is_unsigned && unlikely(val < 0)) ?
07593                     "can't convert negative value to unsigned char" :
07594                     "value too large to convert to unsigned char");
07595             }
07596             return (unsigned char)-1;
07597         }
07598         return (unsigned char)val;
07599     }
07600     return (unsigned char)__Pyx_PyInt_AsUnsignedLong(x);
07601 }

07774 static CYTHON_INLINE unsigned long __Pyx_PyInt_AsUnsignedLong(PyObject* x) {
07775     const unsigned long neg_one = (unsigned long)-1, const_zero = 0;
07776     const int is_unsigned = neg_one > const_zero;
07777 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x03000000
07778     if (likely(PyInt_Check(x))) {
07779         long val = PyInt_AS_LONG(x);
07780         if (is_unsigned && unlikely(val < 0)) {
07781             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_OverflowError,
07782                             "can't convert negative value to unsigned long");
07783             return (unsigned long)-1;
07784         }
07785         return (unsigned long)val;
07786     } else
07787 #endif
07788     if (likely(PyLong_Check(x))) {
07789         if (is_unsigned) {
07790             if (unlikely(Py_SIZE(x) < 0)) {
07791                 PyErr_SetString(PyExc_OverflowError,
07792                                 "can't convert negative value to unsigned long");
07793                 return (unsigned long)-1;
07794             }
07795             return (unsigned long)PyLong_AsUnsignedLong(x);
07796         } else {
07797             return (unsigned long)PyLong_AsLong(x);
07798         }
07799     } else {
07800         unsigned long val;
07801         PyObject *tmp = __Pyx_PyNumber_Int(x);
07802         if (!tmp) return (unsigned long)-1;
07803         val = __Pyx_PyInt_AsUnsignedLong(tmp);
07804         Py_DECREF(tmp);
07805         return val;
07806     }
07807 }

07984 static int __Pyx_check_binary_version(void) {
07985     char ctversion[4], rtversion[4];
07986     PyOS_snprintf(ctversion, 4, "%d.%d", PY_MAJOR_VERSION, PY_MINOR_VERSION);
07987     PyOS_snprintf(rtversion, 4, "%s", Py_GetVersion());
07988     if (ctversion[0] != rtversion[0] || ctversion[2] != rtversion[2]) {
07989         char message[200];
07990         PyOS_snprintf(message, sizeof(message),
07991                       "compiletime version %s of module '%.100s' "
07992                       "does not match runtime version %s",
07993                       ctversion, __Pyx_MODULE_NAME, rtversion);
07994         #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
07995         return PyErr_Warn(NULL, message);
07996         #else
07997         return PyErr_WarnEx(NULL, message, 1);
07998         #endif
07999     }
08000     return 0;
08001 }
08002 
08003 #ifndef __PYX_HAVE_RT_ImportType
08004 #define __PYX_HAVE_RT_ImportType
08005 static PyTypeObject *__Pyx_ImportType(const char *module_name, const char *class_name,
08006     size_t size, int strict)
08007 {
08008     PyObject *py_module = 0;
08009     PyObject *result = 0;
08010     PyObject *py_name = 0;
08011     char warning[200];
08012 
08013     py_module = __Pyx_ImportModule(module_name);
08014     if (!py_module)
08015         goto bad;
08016     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
08017     py_name = PyString_FromString(class_name);
08018     #else
08019     py_name = PyUnicode_FromString(class_name);
08020     #endif
08021     if (!py_name)
08022         goto bad;
08023     result = PyObject_GetAttr(py_module, py_name);
08024     Py_DECREF(py_name);
08025     py_name = 0;
08026     Py_DECREF(py_module);
08027     py_module = 0;
08028     if (!result)
08029         goto bad;
08030     if (!PyType_Check(result)) {
08031         PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
08032             "%s.%s is not a type object",
08033             module_name, class_name);
08034         goto bad;
08035     }
08036     if (!strict && ((PyTypeObject *)result)->tp_basicsize > (Py_ssize_t)size) {
08037         PyOS_snprintf(warning, sizeof(warning),
08038             "%s.%s size changed, may indicate binary incompatibility",
08039             module_name, class_name);
08040         #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
08041         if (PyErr_Warn(NULL, warning) < 0) goto bad;
08042         #else
08043         if (PyErr_WarnEx(NULL, warning, 0) < 0) goto bad;
08044         #endif
08045     }
08046     else if (((PyTypeObject *)result)->tp_basicsize != (Py_ssize_t)size) {
08047         PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
08048             "%s.%s has the wrong size, try recompiling",
08049             module_name, class_name);
08050         goto bad;
08051     }
08052     return (PyTypeObject *)result;
08053 bad:
08054     Py_XDECREF(py_module);
08055     Py_XDECREF(result);
08056     return NULL;
08057 }
08058 #endif
08059 
08060 #ifndef __PYX_HAVE_RT_ImportModule
08061 #define __PYX_HAVE_RT_ImportModule
08062 static PyObject *__Pyx_ImportModule(const char *name) {
08063     PyObject *py_name = 0;
08064     PyObject *py_module = 0;
08065 
08066     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
08067     py_name = PyString_FromString(name);
08068     #else
08069     py_name = PyUnicode_FromString(name);
08070     #endif
08071     if (!py_name)
08072         goto bad;
08073     py_module = PyImport_Import(py_name);
08074     Py_DECREF(py_name);
08075     return py_module;
08076 bad:
08077     Py_XDECREF(py_name);
08078     return 0;
08079 }
08080 #endif
08081 
08082 #include "compile.h"
08083 #include "frameobject.h"
08084 #include "traceback.h"
08085 
08086 static void __Pyx_AddTraceback(const char *funcname, int __pyx_clineno,
08087                                int __pyx_lineno, const char *__pyx_filename) {
08088     PyObject *py_srcfile = 0;
08089     PyObject *py_funcname = 0;
08090     PyObject *py_globals = 0;
08091     PyCodeObject *py_code = 0;
08092     PyFrameObject *py_frame = 0;
08093 
08094     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
08095     py_srcfile = PyString_FromString(__pyx_filename);
08096     #else
08097     py_srcfile = PyUnicode_FromString(__pyx_filename);
08098     #endif
08099     if (!py_srcfile) goto bad;
08100     if (__pyx_clineno) {
08101         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
08102         py_funcname = PyString_FromFormat( "%s (%s:%d)", funcname, __pyx_cfilenm, __pyx_clineno);
08103         #else
08104         py_funcname = PyUnicode_FromFormat( "%s (%s:%d)", funcname, __pyx_cfilenm, __pyx_clineno);
08105         #endif
08106     }
08107     else {
08108         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
08109         py_funcname = PyString_FromString(funcname);
08110         #else
08111         py_funcname = PyUnicode_FromString(funcname);
08112         #endif
08113     }
08114     if (!py_funcname) goto bad;
08115     py_globals = PyModule_GetDict(__pyx_m);
08116     if (!py_globals) goto bad;
08117     py_code = PyCode_New(
08118         0,            /*int argcount,*/
08119         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
08120         0,            /*int kwonlyargcount,*/
08121         #endif
08122         0,            /*int nlocals,*/
08123         0,            /*int stacksize,*/
08124         0,            /*int flags,*/
08125         __pyx_empty_bytes, /*PyObject *code,*/
08126         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *consts,*/
08127         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *names,*/
08128         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *varnames,*/
08129         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *freevars,*/
08130         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *cellvars,*/
08131         py_srcfile,   /*PyObject *filename,*/
08132         py_funcname,  /*PyObject *name,*/
08133         __pyx_lineno,   /*int firstlineno,*/
08134         __pyx_empty_bytes  /*PyObject *lnotab*/
08135     );
08136     if (!py_code) goto bad;
08137     py_frame = PyFrame_New(
08138         PyThreadState_GET(), /*PyThreadState *tstate,*/
08139         py_code,             /*PyCodeObject *code,*/
08140         py_globals,          /*PyObject *globals,*/
08141         0                    /*PyObject *locals*/
08142     );
08143     if (!py_frame) goto bad;
08144     py_frame->f_lineno = __pyx_lineno;
08145     PyTraceBack_Here(py_frame);
08146 bad:
08147     Py_XDECREF(py_srcfile);
08148     Py_XDECREF(py_funcname);
08149     Py_XDECREF(py_code);
08150     Py_XDECREF(py_frame);
08151 }
08152 
08153 static int __Pyx_InitStrings(__Pyx_StringTabEntry *t) {
08154     while (t->p) {
08155         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
08156         if (t->is_unicode) {
08157             *t->p = PyUnicode_DecodeUTF8(t->s, t->n - 1, NULL);
08158         } else if (t->intern) {
08159             *t->p = PyString_InternFromString(t->s);
08160         } else {
08161             *t->p = PyString_FromStringAndSize(t->s, t->n - 1);
08162         }
08163         #else  /* Python 3+ has unicode identifiers */
08164         if (t->is_unicode | t->is_str) {
08165             if (t->intern) {
08166                 *t->p = PyUnicode_InternFromString(t->s);
08167             } else if (t->encoding) {
08168                 *t->p = PyUnicode_Decode(t->s, t->n - 1, t->encoding, NULL);
08169             } else {
08170                 *t->p = PyUnicode_FromStringAndSize(t->s, t->n - 1);
08171             }
08172         } else {
08173             *t->p = PyBytes_FromStringAndSize(t->s, t->n - 1);
08174         }
08175         #endif
08176         if (!*t->p)
08177             return -1;
08178         ++t;
08179     }
08180     return 0;
08181 }

08185 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_PyObject_IsTrue(PyObject* x) {
08186    int is_true = x == Py_True;
08187    if (is_true | (x == Py_False) | (x == Py_None)) return is_true;
08188    else return PyObject_IsTrue(x);
08189 }
08190 
08191 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject* __Pyx_PyNumber_Int(PyObject* x) {
08192   PyNumberMethods *m;
08193   const char *name = NULL;
08194   PyObject *res = NULL;
08195 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x03000000
08196   if (PyInt_Check(x) || PyLong_Check(x))
08197 #else
08198   if (PyLong_Check(x))
08199 #endif
08200     return Py_INCREF(x), x;
08201   m = Py_TYPE(x)->tp_as_number;
08202 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x03000000
08203   if (m && m->nb_int) {
08204     name = "int";
08205     res = PyNumber_Int(x);
08206   }
08207   else if (m && m->nb_long) {
08208     name = "long";
08209     res = PyNumber_Long(x);
08210   }
08211 #else
08212   if (m && m->nb_int) {
08213     name = "int";
08214     res = PyNumber_Long(x);
08215   }
08216 #endif
08217   if (res) {
08218 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x03000000
08219     if (!PyInt_Check(res) && !PyLong_Check(res)) {
08220 #else
08221     if (!PyLong_Check(res)) {
08222 #endif
08223       PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
08224                    "__%s__ returned non-%s (type %.200s)",
08225                    name, name, Py_TYPE(res)->tp_name);
08226       Py_DECREF(res);
08227       return NULL;
08228     }
08229   }
08230   else if (!PyErr_Occurred()) {
08231     PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
08232                     "an integer is required");
08233   }
08234   return res;
08235 }
08236 
08237 static CYTHON_INLINE Py_ssize_t __Pyx_PyIndex_AsSsize_t(PyObject* b) {
08238   Py_ssize_t ival;
08239   PyObject* x = PyNumber_Index(b);
08240   if (!x) return -1;
08241   ival = PyInt_AsSsize_t(x);
08242   Py_DECREF(x);
08243   return ival;
08244 }
08245 
08246 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject * __Pyx_PyInt_FromSize_t(size_t ival) {
08247 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
08248    if (ival <= LONG_MAX)
08249        return PyInt_FromLong((long)ival);
08250    else {
08251        unsigned char *bytes = (unsigned char *) &ival;
08252        int one = 1; int little = (int)*(unsigned char*)&one;
08253        return _PyLong_FromByteArray(bytes, sizeof(size_t), little, 0);
08254    }
08255 #else
08256    return PyInt_FromSize_t(ival);
08257 #endif
08258 }
08259 
08260 static CYTHON_INLINE size_t __Pyx_PyInt_AsSize_t(PyObject* x) {
08261    unsigned PY_LONG_LONG val = __Pyx_PyInt_AsUnsignedLongLong(x);
08262    if (unlikely(val == (unsigned PY_LONG_LONG)-1 && PyErr_Occurred())) {
08263        return (size_t)-1;
08264    } else if (unlikely(val != (unsigned PY_LONG_LONG)(size_t)val)) {
08265        PyErr_SetString(PyExc_OverflowError,
08266                        "value too large to convert to size_t");
08267        return (size_t)-1;
08268    }
08269    return (size_t)val;
08270 }
